 1023         END IF;
 1024       END IF;
 1025     END PROCESS Delay17_process;

 1150         END IF;
 1151       END IF;

 1171     Delay1_process : PROCESS (clk)

 5257     
 5258     Compare_To_Zero_out1_4 <= '1' WHEN if_bitget_Mant_tmp_Mant_tmp_Wor_out1 = to_unsigned(16#00#, 8) ELSE
 5259         '0';
 5260   
 5261     Logical_Operator_out1_9 <= Compare_To_Zero_out1_4 OR BitSlice2_out1_2;
 5262   
 5263     BitSlice3_out1_2 <= if_bitget_Mant_tmp_1_0_out1(23 DOWNTO 1);
 5264   
 5265     C_out1_19 <= to_unsigned(16#000000#, 23);
 5266   
 5267     
 5268     if_bitget_Mant_tmp_Mant_tmp_Wor_1_out1 <= BitSlice3_out1_2 WHEN Logical_Operator_out1_9 = '0' ELSE
 5269         C_out1_19;
 5270   
 5271     Constant1_out1_1 <= to_unsigned(16#000000#, 23);
 5272   
 5273     Constant3_out1_2 <= to_unsigned(16#400000#, 23);
 5274   
 5275     
 5276     Switch3_out1_1 <= Constant1_out1_1 WHEN Logical_Operator1_out1_4 = '0' ELSE
 5277         Constant3_out1_2;
 5278   
 5279     
 5280     Switch1_out1_16 <= Switch3_out1_1 WHEN Logical_Operator_out1_8 = '0' ELSE
 5281         checkDenormal_out2;
 5282   
 5283     Delay19_4_process : PROCESS (clk)
 5284     BEGIN
 5285       IF clk'EVENT AND clk = '1' THEN
 5286         IF reset = '1' THEN
 5287           Delay19_reg_1(0) <= to_unsigned(16#000000#, 23);
 5288           Delay19_reg_1(1) <= to_unsigned(16#000000#, 23);
 5289           Delay19_reg_1(2) <= to_unsigned(16#000000#, 23);
 5290           Delay19_reg_1(3) <= to_unsigned(16#000000#, 23);
 5291           Delay19_reg_1(4) <= to_unsigned(16#000000#, 23);
 5292           Delay19_reg_1(5) <= to_unsigned(16#000000#, 23);
 5293           Delay19_reg_1(6) <= to_unsigned(16#000000#, 23);
 5294           Delay19_reg_1(7) <= to_unsigned(16#000000#, 23);
 5295           Delay19_reg_1(8) <= to_unsigned(16#000000#, 23);
 5296           Delay19_reg_1(9) <= to_unsigned(16#000000#, 23);
 5297           Delay19_reg_1(10) <= to_unsigned(16#000000#, 23);
 5298           Delay19_reg_1(11) <= to_unsigned(16#000000#, 23);
 5299         ELSIF enb = '1' THEN
 5300           Delay19_reg_1(0) <= Delay19_reg_next_1(0);
 5301           Delay19_reg_1(1) <= Delay19_reg_next_1(1);
 5302           Delay19_reg_1(2) <= Delay19_reg_next_1(2);
 5303           Delay19_reg_1(3) <= Delay19_reg_next_1(3);
 5304           Delay19_reg_1(4) <= Delay19_reg_next_1(4);
 5305           Delay19_reg_1(5) <= Delay19_reg_next_1(5);
 5306           Delay19_reg_1(6) <= Delay19_reg_next_1(6);
 5307           Delay19_reg_1(7) <= Delay19_reg_next_1(7);
 5308           Delay19_reg_1(8) <= Delay19_reg_next_1(8);
 5309           Delay19_reg_1(9) <= Delay19_reg_next_1(9);
 5310           Delay19_reg_1(10) <= Delay19_reg_next_1(10);
 5311           Delay19_reg_1(11) <= Delay19_reg_next_1(11);
 5312         END IF;
 5313       END IF;
 5314     END PROCESS Delay19_4_process;
 5315   
 5316     Delay19_out1_4 <= Delay19_reg_1(11);
 5317     Delay19_reg_next_1(0) <= Switch1_out1_16;
 5318     Delay19_reg_next_1(1) <= Delay19_reg_1(0);
 5319     Delay19_reg_next_1(2) <= Delay19_reg_1(1);
 5320     Delay19_reg_next_1(3) <= Delay19_reg_1(2);
 5321     Delay19_reg_next_1(4) <= Delay19_reg_1(3);
 5322     Delay19_reg_next_1(5) <= Delay19_reg_1(4);
 5323     Delay19_reg_next_1(6) <= Delay19_reg_1(5);
 5324     Delay19_reg_next_1(7) <= Delay19_reg_1(6);
 5325     Delay19_reg_next_1(8) <= Delay19_reg_1(7);
 5326     Delay19_reg_next_1(9) <= Delay19_reg_1(8);
 5327     Delay19_reg_next_1(10) <= Delay19_reg_1(9);
 5328     Delay19_reg_next_1(11) <= Delay19_reg_1(10);
 5329   
 5330     
 5331     if_rem_Exceptional_Check_cfType_1_out1 <= if_bitget_Mant_tmp_Mant_tmp_Wor_1_out1 WHEN Delay20_out1 = '0' ELSE
 5332         Delay19_out1_4;
 5333   
 5334     
 5335     Switch5_out1_1 <= Constant2_out1_2 WHEN Relational_Operator_relop1 = '0' ELSE
 5336         if_rem_Exceptional_Check_cfType_1_out1;
 5337   
 5338     Delay7_6_process : PROCESS (clk)
 5339     BEGIN
 5340       IF clk'EVENT AND clk = '1' THEN
 5341         IF reset = '1' THEN
 5342           Delay7_out1_6 <= to_unsigned(16#000000#, 23);
 5343         ELSIF enb = '1' THEN
 5344           Delay7_out1_6 <= Switch5_out1_1;
 5345         END IF;
 5346       END IF;
 5347     END PROCESS Delay7_6_process;
 5348   
 5349   
 5350     -- Combine FP sign, exponent, mantissa into 32 bit word
 5351     nfp_out_pack <= Delay5_out1 & Delay6_out1_6 & Delay7_out1_6;
 5352   
 5353     nfp_out <= std_logic_vector(nfp_out_pack);
 5354   
 5355   END rtl;
